// Client provides and manages an etcd v3 client session.\\n51: type Client struct {\\n52: \\tCluster\\n53: \\tKV\\n54: \\tLease\\n55: \\tWatcher\\n56: \\tAuth\\n57: \\tMaintenance\\n58: \\n59:
